< Text>
Oh-my-goodness!!!! Ever since my boyfriend and I experienced the beauty of Cuban food in Florida we've been on the hunt everywhere we go. So of course on our trip down to LA we scoured and found this incredible gem. We tried the beef empanadas, vacas fritas, ropa vieja and a pitcher of sangria to wash it down. Everything was absolutely amazing... but the empanadas are what I will dream about until my next visit to LA. They are so big, delicious, savory and well balanced. They have earned a place on my must do's whenever I visit LA, and I highly recommend you give them a try!!< /Text>

<Gmap_id>0x808561fa03a1c44b:0xc700f368f784f78b</Gmap_id><review>1/19/15

A rabbit hopped into my life at the beginning of the year. I own a condo with two cats and a husband so I didn't really need another pet to clean up after, but the poor little thing was terrified when we brought her in. I found a large hutch on Craigslist and asked the seller where he took his rabbits: he recommended VCA for exotic pets and told me about the free first visit.

I brought in little Clarice after a week of falling in love with her. I guess I should have looked a little closer under her tail, because I was a little disappointed to learn at the visit that Clarice was actually a boy rabbit. So now her... err, his name is Clarence. Dr. Garrow answered the list of questions I brought with me. Gina was also very knowledgeable and happy to talk rabbit with me.

My biggest concern at the visit was fleas. I think the rabbit brought some home with her, so they gave me one month free of prescription Revolution. I asked about my cats and decided to refill their Advantage online (and was told to make sure the rabbit doesn't get Advantage). No problem - I'll come back here for two more months of rabbit Revolution to make sure we don't end up with more "pets" than we want in the house. Fleas not welcome!

The visit wasn't rushed and they were on time. I am new at being a bunny mom, but so far I have found that Clarence loves to roam around our house, chase the felines, and give big bunny kisses all over my face. He steals sips of my husbands Kool-Aid when he's being bad, but for the most part is a good rabbit and he's happy with his new home.< /review>< Rating>
5< /Rating>

<user>109120346587306607618</user>< name>
Mike Richardson<//name>
<Date>1615586495649<//Date><Rate>5<//Rate>< review>
Grizzly Ranch is hands down my favorite course in all of Reno/Tahoe (I've lived in Reno since 2003). In the summer of 2020 my family and I bought a second home on the 9th hole and it was the best decision we've ever made. Having a home that is outdoors and on a golf course, yet is still only 45 minutes away from Reno where we call home, is absolutely amazing.

The golf course, though challenging, is very forgiving for the average golfer, which makes it fun every single time I play. Prior to purchasing my home I regretfully had never played the course before. After playing that first time I think I was able to play 15+ more times throughout the rest of the season. I have 3 small children, so being able to introduce them to golf and having them learn how to play at Grizzly is something I am very much looking forward to. Every single person I have brought along with me for the weekend is absolutely blown away that this magnificent course is right in our backyard. The course layout, the amenities, the staff...everything is absolutely amazing!

For anyone considering getting a place up in this area...do it! I promise you won't regret it.< /review>

< text>
Save your money...They don't tell you the condition of the course when you book a tee time "not good". In addition they over book and as a a matter of fact you need a book while you wait to play the next whole. Don't bother mentioning the pain to the pro shop they have every excuse in the book plus Sam is NOT your friend. All they could tell me is they have a problem with water for the course and this upcoming year is obviously unfortunately going to be an additional issue for them. Don't get me wrong, I love this track and typically prime time just not right now. Wait at least a month to play on something half way decent especially for the money they charge. If you go between now and a month from now be prepared for unfavorable conditions and slow days with no consideration of keeping the pace of play moving.

The dragon postponed there opening from the 14th to the 26th of this month because the course wasn't ready, neither is the Grizzly but they need the money I guess.

No Dragon is not anything close to the Grizzly, my point is when you charge full boat disclose or give us a break based on the conditions, surprises are a huge drag for us golf folk.<//text>

< review>
Caleb and staff in the pro shop are great! Had a 2:50 tee time on a Friday and they gave us the 9 hole rate. The course is a very fair track with multiple tees for all skill levels. Very picturesque and some stunning views. My only reason for not giving 5 stars was the condition of the traps (very little sand, kinda like hitting off hard pavement, and some were not raked by previous players). The greens rolled true but then again, ball marks were all over and not repaired. Need to do that to keep this course in top shape. Got finished at sunset, and overall a very good experience. If you get the chance to play, dont pass it up. Peace</review>

We had a good experience over all but there are definitely a lot of things that were not OK.
The bathrooms and  the facilities were absolutely disgusting. We used the adult shower in the Ibachi lodge and that was the "nicest" one! Nasty!
The food was very pleasant for camp food. I will have to say the portions were not enough to keep a growing boy from being hungry. If you were to look at standard portion sizes they were not met in any of the categories. ( There was a rumor it was because of other troops deciding not to make their own food)
Their trail to 1st class director was not necessarily is somebody appropriate for that position. Very nice sky but just not the right knowledge for that particular job. There were several times while " teaching " the kids different things he was wrong!
Their handicraft area was staffed absolutely amazingly. I recommended to one of the young kids and their that maybe he possibly take the position for trail to 1st classed next year. He was super great with the kids even the ones with special needs
My review sounds like it was all bad but the kids had an absolutely amazing time and the camp over all was a very beautiful place.</text>

<review>While the location is absolutely beautiful, the good things about the camp fall off quickly from there. Some staff members were great while others were rude to the boys, and the meals left much to be desired with raw chicken being served once. More agregious, however, is the severe lack of coordination and direction by the camp's director. Councilors had incorrect schedules for their classes, important information was not always conveyed clearly, and nobody either had or were willing to use their radios to communicate questions to the staff members that could answer questions,causing regular confusion.

With how gorgeous the location is, these limitations are a tragedy to the camp, and hopefully they can find a director better capable of managing the operations to allow the camp to shine.</review>< Gmap_id>

Not only is that VERY annoying for those of us who listen to audible (via the phone) or sirius (also via my phone) but it is a MAJOR SAFETY issue.  The point of a connection is so you have hands free and not fooling around with the bloody phone while driving.  And no, some of us don't wear ear pieces or headsets for legitimate reasons.   The car computer should either keep the "connect" once made (it worked once I did the connection -- until signal was lost in a valley/ dead zone or I stopped the car.  Then I had to reconnect all over again).  And the connection ought to be easy (a hand out would be nice, because every car is just a bit different).  God forbid if I'd needed to call 911.  Check in -- i could have brought the car in earlier if you had better hours, but nope.  otherwise that also was ok although the specific Enterprise location could stand to have some more parking space.   SO 3 stars and, despite my MANY years of using Enterprise, I may well be looking at a different car rental company the next time out.< /Text>

This place is great. It‚Äôs family owned, the vibes are welcoming and friendly, and the food is delicious, huge portions, and cheap.

You order at the counter and then find a table outside, and they‚Äôll bring you out your food. They also start you off by bringing you some fresh chips and salsa, which had a good amount of kick to it but wasn‚Äôt overly spicy.

My partner got the Chile Verde Fat Burrito and it was really great‚Äîloved the amount of variety you could get with burritos. It‚Äôs about the size of your face and so well priced for how much food it is.

A very tasty road trip takeout experience!

We ordered:
- 2 giant burritos (carne asada)
- 3 tacos (al pastor, carne asada, carnitas)
- 1 flautas plate (chicken)
- 1 tostada (carne asada)

My husband and father-in-law both enjoyed the carne asada! They both said it was excellent.

The chicken flautas were my favorite. They were covered in guac and sour cream. So tasty. Perfect crispy crunch. Not too oily. The beans had a soft, buttery texture. The rice was okay too.

Of the two tacos I had, I preferred the al pastor over the carnitas. The homemade tortillas though were the star of the show! So delicious!

The employees were also so friendly and helpful. We will be coming back again on our next road trip :)< /text>

< Text>
Hands down the best Mexican food in Gilroy. Nobody believes me until they go, and then they say "OMG that is the best Mexican food in Gilroy."  Family run, the grandfather makes all of the sauces. Oh, and did I tell you about the homemade corn tortillas?????? JUST GO. Thank me later. We had them cater our wedding in 2013, and everyone said it was the best wedding food they'd ever had, and thanked us for not doing a prime rib buffet. We've moved, and miss this place terribly.<//Text>
